Here is the situation:\\ \tt \\ \tt WHAT: Things at places\\ \tt LEFT: books\\ \tt RIGHT: bowl\\ \tt TOP: suit\\ \tt BOTTOM: spoons\\ \tt CENTER: nuts\\ \tt NORTHWEST: bolt\\ \tt NORTHEAST: narcissus\\ \tt SOUTHWEST: violet\\ \tt SOUTHEAST: copper\\ \tt HERE: tiger\\ \tt THERE: camellia\\ \tt NOWHERE: eye shadow\\ \tt EVERYWHERE: ladder\\ \tt INSIDE: chalk\\ \tt OUTSIDE: tambourine\\ \tt \\ \tt Questions from the questioner will start with QUESTIONER. Please reply in the form: ANSWER: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt I will also ask you questions. These questions will start with ME: . Please answer these questions with: ASIDE: <some text>\\ \tt \\ \tt Important: Give short, direct answers!\\ \tt \\ \tt Let us start.

	   }
